<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Fra Holbergs tid, Suite i gammel stil
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Aus Holbergs Zeit, Suite im alten Stil&#160;; From Holberg's Time, Holberg Suite
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Grieg,_Edvard" title="Category:Grieg, Edvard">Grieg, Edvard</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.40
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IEG 33
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements:
<ol><li> Praeludium
</li><li> Sarabande
</li><li> Gavotte
</li><li> Air
</li><li> Rigaudon
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1884
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Erika Lie-Nissen
</td></tr>
<tr>

<tr>
<th>Piece Style

<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>

</th>
<td>piano
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holberg_Suite" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Holberg Suite">Wikipedia article</a><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.sheetmusicplus.com/composers/edvard-grieg-sheet-music/1800439?Ntt=Holberg&amp;narrow_by=Holberg&amp;Ns=default&amp;recsPerPage=50&amp;id=298930"><i>Holberg Suite</i> - scores at Sheet Music Plus</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Commissioned for a commemoration of the 200th anniversary of Ludwig Holberg's birth
</td></tr></table>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>The work is originally for piano, although the composer's arrangement for string orchestra is more well-known.
</li></ul>
